    <td style="text-align: justify"><span style="font-size: 10pt">Emerging growth company</span></td></tr>

copy of the press release is furnished herewith as Exhibit 99.1.</p>

that section, and they shall not be deemed incorporated by reference in any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the
Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. The Company is making reference to non-GAAP
financial information in the press release. A reconciliation of the non-GAAP financial measures to the comparable GAAP financial measures
is contained in the attached press release.&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B>Exela Technologies,&nbsp;Inc. Reports Preliminary Second Quarter
2022 Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">August&nbsp;09, 2022 16:05 ET&nbsp;| Source:&nbsp;<U>Exela Technologies,&nbsp;Inc</U>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>



<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><DIV STYLE="margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0; width: 100%"><DIV STYLE="font-size: 1pt; border-top: Black 1pt solid">&nbsp;</DIV></DIV><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

Q2 2021 and DrySign&reg; users growing 1,786% over Q2 2021</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD>Raised $58.2 million through equity offering</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD>Liquidity of $72 million as of June&nbsp;30, 2022</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: left; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt">Conference call scheduled for August&nbsp;9, 2022 at 4:30 PM ET</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">IRVING, Texas, Aug.&nbsp;09, 2022 (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- Exela Technologies,&nbsp;Inc.
(&ldquo;Exela&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;) (NASDAQ: XELA, XELAP), a global business process automation (&ldquo;BPA&rdquo;) leader,
announced today its financial results for the second quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;We started the implementation of the next step of our Capital
Deployment Strategy in Q2. Our capital structure dislocation represents an opportunity to deploy capital from the sale of assets and equity
capital markets to purchase debt and invest for growth. Our business is prepared for tomorrow with tenured management and many additional
new leaders with fresh ideas, who together are working on improving operating results while combating headwinds from the strong dollar,
tight job markets, inflation and a network outage,&rdquo; said Par Chadha, Executive Chairman of Exela.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&ldquo;We are executing well against our growth initiatives and capital
redeployment strategy that enable us to better serve our customers and enhance shareholder value.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><B><U>Second Quarter Highlights</U></B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Revenue:&nbsp;</B>Revenue for Q2 2022 was $266.8 million, a decline of 9.0% compared to $293.0 million in Q2 2021.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.75in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD>Revenue for the ITPS segment was $190.0 million, a decline of 12.6% year-over-year, primarily due to a network outage<SUP>(4)</SUP>,
staffing shortages and the strong dollar.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.75in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD>Healthcare Solutions revenue was $56.4 million, roughly flat year-over-year.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.75in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD>Legal and Loss Prevention Services revenue was $20.4 million, an increase of 4.3% year-over-year.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Operating income/(loss):&nbsp;</B>Operating loss for Q2 2022 was $20.9 million, compared with operating income of $25.4 million
in Q2 2021. The year-over-year increase in operating loss was primarily attributable to lower revenue and higher SG&amp;A spend.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Net Loss:&nbsp;</B>Net loss for Q2 2022 was $79.2 million, compared with a net loss of $19.4 million in Q2 2021.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-indent: -0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.75in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>EBITDA<SUP>(5)</SUP>:&nbsp;</B>EBITDA for Q2 2022 was $(17.6) million compared to $44.9 million in Q2 2021. EBITDA margin for Q2
2022 was (6.6%) compared to 15.3% in Q2 2021.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1pt solid"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->


<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.75in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Adjusted</B>&nbsp;<B>EBITDA<SUP>(6)</SUP>:&nbsp;</B>Adjusted EBITDA for Q2 2022 was $36.5 million, a decrease of 28% compared to
$50.9 million in Q2 2021. Adjusted EBITDA margin for Q2 2022 was 13.7%, a decrease of 371 basis points from 17.4% in Q2 2021 and up from
12.9% in Q1 2022.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Capital Expenditures:&nbsp;</B>Capital expenditures for Q2 2022 were 1.4% of revenue compared to 0.7% of revenue in Q2 2021.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%" STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 0.25in"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">&bull;</FONT></TD><TD><B>Common Stock:</B>&nbsp;As of June&nbsp;30, 2022, there were 40.4 million total shares<SUP>(7)</SUP>.</TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Balance
Sheet and Liquidity</B></FONT>: As of June&nbsp;30, 2022, total liquidity was $72 million. Total net debt<SUP>(8)</SUP>&nbsp;at June&nbsp;30,
2022 was $1.04 billion.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>Expanding
financial flexibility:&nbsp;</B></FONT>Raised a total of $58.2 million in gross proceeds from equity offerings in Q2 2022. In accordance
with Exela's plan to strategically reduce debt and associated interest expense as well as to invest in growth, total debt<SUP>(3)</SUP>&nbsp;was
reduced by $118 million compared to Q1 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>Below
are the notes referenced above:</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>(1)&nbsp;Total Contract Value</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>(2)&nbsp;Digital Mailroom</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>(3)&nbsp;Total
debt includes all long-term debt and interest-bearing current liabilities.</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><I>&nbsp;</I></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>(4)&nbsp;In late June&nbsp;2022, the Company experienced a network
security incident impacting certain of the Company&rsquo;s operational and information technology systems. The Company immediately took
steps to isolate the impact and prevent additional systems from being affected, including taking large parts of its network offline as
a precaution and thereby disrupting some access to our applications and services by our employees and customers. The Company&rsquo;s
systems recovery efforts are substantially complete, and the Company&rsquo;s operations are fully functional, however, the incident did
result in some loss of revenue in the end of the second quarter as well as certain incremental costs, some of which is expected to continue.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>(5)&nbsp;EBITDA is a non-GAAP measure. A reconciliation of EBITDA
is attached to this release.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>(6)&nbsp;Adjusted EBITDA is a non-GAAP measure. A reconciliation
of Adjusted EBITDA is attached to this release.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>(7)&nbsp;On July&nbsp;25, 2022, we effected a one-for-twenty reverse
split (the &ldquo;Reverse Stock Split&rdquo;) of our issued and outstanding shares of common stock, par value $0.0001 per share (&ldquo;Common
Stock&rdquo;). All information related to Common Stock, have been retroactively adjusted to give effect to the Reverse Stock Split.</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>&nbsp;</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><I>(8)&nbsp;Net
debt is calculated as Total debt (excluding the secured debt repurchase facility) less unrestricted cash</I></P>

Results</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B></B></FONT>The financial results described above are preliminary, unaudited and represent the most recent current information
available to&nbsp;Exela&nbsp;management. Exela&rsquo;s actual results may differ from these estimated financial results, including due
to the completion of its financial closing procedures, final adjustments that may arise between the date of this press release and the
time that financial results for the second quarter of 2022 are finalized, and such differences may be material. In addition, these financial
results do not reflect important limitations, qualifications and details that will be included in the full financial statements to be
included in the Company&rsquo;s Form&nbsp;10-Q to be filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;).</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
Exela</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B></B></FONT>Exela Technologies is a business process automation (BPA) leader, leveraging a global footprint and proprietary technology
to provide digital transformation solutions enhancing quality, productivity, and end-user experience. With decades of experience operating
mission-critical processes, Exela serves a growing roster of more than 4,000 customers throughout 50 countries, including over 60% of
the Fortune&reg; 100. Utilizing foundational technologies spanning information management, workflow automation, and integrated communications,
Exela&rsquo;s software and services include multi-industry, departmental solution suites addressing finance and accounting, human capital
management, and legal management, as well as industry-specific solutions for banking, healthcare, insurance, and the public sector. Through
cloud-enabled platforms, built on a configurable stack of automation modules, and approximately 17,000 employees operating in 21 countries,
Exela rapidly deploys integrated technology and operations as an end-to-end digital journey partner.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">Find out more at&nbsp;<U>www.exelatech.com</U></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">To automatically receive Exela financial news by e-mail, please visit
the Exela Investor Relations website,&nbsp;<U>http://investors.exelatech.com/</U>, and subscribe to E-mail Alerts.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><B>About
Non-GAAP Financial Measures:</B></FONT>&nbsp;This press release includes constant currency, EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA, each of which
is a financial measure that is not prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (&ldquo;GAAP&rdquo;). Exela
believes that the presentation of these non-GAAP financial measures will provide useful information to investors in assessing our financial
performance, results of operations and liquidity and allows investors to better understand the trends in our business and to better understand
and compare our results. Exela&rsquo;s board of directors and management use constant currency, EBITDA and Adjusted EBITDA to assess Exela&rsquo;s
financial performance, because it allows them to compare Exela&rsquo;s operating performance on a consistent basis across periods by removing
the effects of Exela&rsquo;s capital structure (such as varying levels of debt and interest expense, as well as transaction costs resulting
from the combination of Quinpario Acquisition Corp. 2, SourceHOV Holdings,&nbsp;Inc. and Novitex Holdings,&nbsp;Inc. on July&nbsp;12,
2017 (the &ldquo;Novitex Business Combination&rdquo;) and capital markets-based activities). Adjusted EBITDA also seeks to remove the
effects of&nbsp;integration&nbsp;and related costs to achieve the savings, any expected reduction in operating expenses due to the Novitex
Business Combination, asset base (such as depreciation and amortization) and other similar non-routine items outside the control of our
management team.&nbsp; Optimization and restructuring expenses and merger adjustments are primarily related to the implementation of strategic
actions and initiatives related to the Novitex Business Combination. All of these costs are variable and dependent upon the nature of
the actions being implemented and can vary significantly driven by business needs. Accordingly, due to that significant variability, we
exclude these charges since we do not believe they truly reflect our past, current or future operating performance. The constant currency
presentation excludes the impact of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates. We calculate constant currency revenue and Adjusted
EBITDA on a constant currency basis by converting our current-period local currency financial results using the exchange rates from the
corresponding prior-period and compare these adjusted amounts to our corresponding prior period reported results. Exela does not consider
these non-GAAP measures in isolation or as an alternative to liquidity or financial measures determined in accordance with GAAP. A limitation
of these non-GAAP financial measures is that they exclude significant expenses and income that are required by GAAP to be recorded in
Exela&rsquo;s financial statements. In addition, they are subject to inherent limitations as they reflect the exercise of judgments by
management about which expenses and income are excluded or included in determining these non-GAAP financial measures and therefore the
basis of presentation for these measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled measures used by other companies. These non-GAAP financial
measures are not required to be uniformly applied, are not audited and should not be considered in isolation or as substitutes for results
prepared in accordance with GAAP. Net loss is the GAAP measure most directly comparable to the non-GAAP measures presented here. For reconciliation
of the comparable GAAP measures to these non-GAAP financial measures, see the schedules attached to this release.</P>
